event = {
	id = 1900
	random = no
	country = REB #(alternatively U56/Vatican)
	persistent = yes
	
	name = "AI_EVENT"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1914 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }

		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = setflag which = theatsAssessed }
		
		command = { type = clrflag which = Threat_level_NA } #North America

		command = { type = clrflag which = Threat_level_AF } #Africa

		#local threat level 5 allows peacetime partial mobilization

			trigger = {

			}

This inevitably means reduction of spending towards other important areas such as healthcare, education, infrastructure, and economic development - critical sectors responsible for our long-term economic growth and social well-being. High military spending can also lead to an increase in national debt, inflation, and gradual impoverishment of our populace. However, if we were to lose a major war or lose our sovereignty to foreign occupation, the consequences could be even more dire. And if we were to achieve victory, on the other hand, the benefits of victory against our rivals could completely outweigh our sacrifices and actually lead to an increase in long-term growth and prosperity. So let us invest in victory!"

	name = "Gearing up for war 3"
	desc = "The rising tensions and conflicts around the world are forcing us to increase our military spending and prepare our industries for another Great War. This inevitably means reduction of spending towards other important areas such as healthcare, education, infrastructure, and economic development - critical sectors responsible for our long-term economic growth and social well-being. High military spending can also lead to an increase in national debt, inflation, and gradual impoverishment of our populace. However, if we were to lose a major war or lose our sovereignty to foreign occupation, the consequences could be even more dire. And if we were to achieve victory, on the other hand, the benefits of victory against our rivals could completely outweigh our sacrifices and actually lead to an increase in long-term growth and prosperity. So let us invest in victory!"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1914 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }

		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR2  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR3  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		
		command = { type = set_domestic which = defense_lobby value = 3 }
		
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes }	type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 3 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = no }	type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = no }	type = local_clrflag which = war_preparedness	 }
		
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR1  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR2  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR3  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR4  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR5  }

		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR10 }
	}

	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR2  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR3  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR4  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR5  } } type = belligerence value = 1 }
		
		command = { type = set_domestic which = defense_lobby value = 5 }
		
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes }	type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 5 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = no }	type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = no }	type = local_clrflag which = war_preparedness	 }
		
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR1  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR2  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR3  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR4  }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = WAR5  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR6  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR7  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR8  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR9  }
		command = { type = local_clrflag which = WAR10 }
	}
}

	id = 2006
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	TAG = { AFG ALB ALG ANG ARA ARG ARM AST AUS AZB BEL BEN BHU BLR BOL BOS BRA BRU BUL BUR CAL CAM CAN CGX CHC CHI CHL CMB COL CON COS CRO CSA CSX CUB CXB CYN CYP CZE DDR DEN DFR DOM EAF ECU EGY ENG EQA EST ETH EUS FIN FLA FRA GAB GEO GER GLD GRE GUA GUI GUY HAI HOL HON HUN ICL IDC IND INO IRE IRQ ISR ITA JAP JOR KAZ KOR KUR KYG LAO LAT LBY LEB LIB LIT LUX MAD MAL MAN MEN MEX MLY MON MOR MOZ MTN NAM NEP NIC NIG NOR NZL OMN OTT PAK PAL PAN PAR PER PHI POL POR PRI PRK PRU QUE RHO ROM RSI RUS SAF SAL SAR SAU SCA SCH SCO SER SIA SIB SIE SIK SLO SLV SOM SOV SPA SPR SUD SWE SYR TAJ TAN TEX TIB TRA TRK TUN TUR UKR URU USA UZB VEN VIE WLL YEM YUG U01 U02 U03 U04 U05 U06 U08 U09 U10 U11 U12 U13 U14 U15 U16 U17 U18 U19 U20 U21 U22 U23 U24 U25 U26 U27 U28 U29 U30 U31 U32 U33 U34 U35 U36 U39 U40 U41 U42 U43 U44 U45 U46 U47 U48 U49 U50 U51 U52 U53 U54 U55 U56 U57 U58 U59 U60 U61 U62 U63 U64 U65 U66 U67 U68 U69 U70 U71 U72 U73 U74 U75 U76 U77 U78 U79 U80 U81 U82 U83 U84 U85 U86 U87 U88 U89 U90 U91 U92 U93 U94 U95 U96 U97 U98 U99 USN UIC UTL UAU UPS UCH UBO UCS URO UER UGS UPE UTC }
	
	trigger = {
		flag = theatsAssessed
		local_flag = AllInit
		policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 5 } 
		NOT = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 6 } } 
		policy = { type = professional_army value = 3 }
		OR = {
			policy = { type = professional_army value = 8 } #General mobilization
			lost_national = { value = 5 } #Invaded
			local_flag = inMajorWar
			AND = {
				continent = "North America"
				OR = {
					AND = {
						policy = { type = interventionism value = 7 } 
						OR = {
							#flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 6 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_SA when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_EU when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_AP when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_AF when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 4 }
						}
					}
					
					#Far away threats
					#flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 8 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_SA when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_EU when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_AP when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_AF when = 1 value = 9 }
					
					#closer to home threats
					flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 6 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				continent = "South America"
				OR = {
					AND = {
						policy = { type = interventionism value = 7 } 
						OR = {
							flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 6 }
							#flag = { which = Threat_level_SA when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_EU when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_AP when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_AF when = 1 value = 7 }
							flag = { which = Threat_level_SA when = 1 value = 4 }
						}
					}
					
					#Far away threats
					flag = { which = Threat_level_NA when = 1 value = 8 }
					#flag = { which = Threat_level_SA when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_EU when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_AP when = 1 value = 9 }
					flag = { which = Threat_level_AF when = 1 value = 9 }

	name = "Gearing up for war 6"
	desc = "The rising tensions and conflicts around the world are forcing us to increase our military spending and prepare our industries for another Great War. This inevitably means reduction of spending towards other important areas such as healthcare, education, infrastructure, and economic development - critical sectors responsible for our long-term economic growth and social well-being. 	#TAG = { AFG ALB ALG ANG ARA ARG ARM AST AUS AZB BEL BEN BHU BLR BOL BOS BRA BRU BUL BUR CAL CAM CAN CGX CHC CHI CHL CMB COL CON COS CRO CSA CSX CUB CXB CYN CYP CZE DDR DEN DFR DOM EAF ECU EGY ENG EQA EST ETH EUS FIN FLA FRA GAB GEO GER GLD GRE GUA GUI GUY HAI HOL HON HUN ICL IDC IND INO IRE IRQ ISR ITA JAP JOR KAZ KOR KUR KYG LAO LAT LBY LEB LIB LIT LUX MAD MAL MAN MEN MEX MLY MON MOR MOZ MTN NAM NEP NIC NIG NOR NZL OMN OTT PAK PAL PAN PAR PER PHI POL POR PRI PRK PRU QUE RHO ROM RSI RUS SAF SAL SAR SAU SCA SCH SCO SER SIA SIB SIE SIK SLO SLV SOM SOV SPA SPR SUD SWE SYR TAJ TAN TEX TIB TRA TRK TUN TUR UKR URU USA UZB VEN VIE WLL YEM YUG U01 U02 U03 U04 U05 U06 U08 U09 U10 U11 U12 U13 U14 U15 U16 U17 U18 U19 U20 U21 U22 U23 U24 U25 U26 U27 U28 U29 U30 U31 U32 U33 U34 U35 U36 U39 U40 U41 U42 U43 U44 U45 U46 U47 U48 U49 U50 U51 U52 U53 U54 U55 U56 U57 U58 U59 U60 U61 U62 U63 U64 U65 U66 U67 U68 U69 U70 U71 U72 U73 U74 U75 U76 U77 U78 U79 U80 U81 U82 U83 U84 U85 U86 U87 U88 U89 U90 U91 U92 U93 U94 U95 U96 U97 U98 U99 USN UIC UTL UAU UPS UCH UBO UCS URO UER UGS UPE UTC }
	
	trigger = {
		local_flag = AllInit
		month = 11
		OR = {
			AND = {
				year = 1936
				NOT = { local_flag = { which = EconomicGrowth when = 1 value = 1936 } }
			}
			AND = {
				year = 1937
				NOT = { local_flag = { which = EconomicGrowth when = 1 value = 1937 } }
			}
			AND = {
				year = 1938
				NOT = { local_flag = { which = EconomicGrowth when = 1 value = 1938 } }
			}

				year = 1939

			}

			}

	name = "Economic growth"
	desc = "Each year our country experiences some natural level of economic growth. This growth rate is partly a factor of historical factors, and partly the result of our current circumstances - such as wars, debt, and economic mobilization policy."
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = december year = 1936 }
	offset = 12
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }
	
	action = {
		name = "Show me the stats for this year"
		command = { type = event which = 3001 where = -1 when = 0 }
	}
}
	
event = {
	id = 3001
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	
	name = "Economic growth"
	desc = EVT_3001_DESC
	style = 2

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		#default 4 percent ic / 2 percent resources
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total	value = 2 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = ic		value = 2 }
		
		#Poorer countries generally have higher growth average, up to +4.5% maximum. 1936 stats:
		#command = { 															   type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.0 }	#+0.0% US/UK/Switzerland/Denmark/NewZealand
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 10 } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+0.5% Germany/France/Netherlands/Sweden
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 9  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+1.0% Canada/Norway/Finland/Argentina
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 8  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+1.5% Italy/Japan/Hungary/Czechosolovakia
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 7  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+2.0% USSR/South Africa/Spain/Greece
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 6  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+2.5% Poland/Portugal/Turkey/Bulgaria
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 5  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+3.0% Yugoslavia/Thailand/Indonesia/Romania
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 4  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+3.5% China/India/Kenya/Nigeria
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 3  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+4.0% Albania/Egypt/Ethiopia/Saudi Arabia
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { policy = { type = freedom value = 2  } } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0.5 }	#+4.5% Afghanistan/Yemen/Oman/Default new country
		
		#Changes before 1939:
		#+1: Germany, USSR, Austria, Poland, Canada, Norway, Finland, Greece, Venezuela
		#-1: Spain, Nicaragua, Singapore
		command = { trigger = { 
						year = 1938 NOT = { year = 1939 }
						OR = {
							country = GER
							country = AUS
							country = POL
							country = CAN
							country = NOR
							country = FIN
							country = GRE
							country = VEN
							AND = { country = SOV local_flag = { which = SOVAmbition_count when = 1 value = 2 } } #At least 2 years worth of forced modernization
						}
					}
					type = domestic which = freedom value = 1 }
					
		command = { trigger = { 
						year = 1938 NOT = { year = 1939 }
						OR = {
							country = NIC
							AND = {
								OR = {
									country = SPA
									country = SPR
									country = EUS
									country = U52
									country = U69
								}
								local_flag = { which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 12 } #War did not end before the end of 1937
							}
						}
					}
					type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
					
	
		
		#Germany and US start with 6
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = Depression	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic			value = 4  }	#Recovering from Great Depression
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = Depression	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = Depression	value = -1 }	#Recovering from Great Depression
		
		#policy-based. At full war mobilization, getting -5.5% yearly growth
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 1  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.1 } #-0.1
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 2  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.2 } #-0.3
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 3  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.3 } #-0.6
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 4  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.4 } #-1.0
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 5  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.5 } #-1.5
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 6  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.6 } #-2.1
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 7  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.7 } #-2.8
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 8  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.8 } #-3.6
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 9  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.9 } #-4.5
		command = { trigger = { policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 10 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1.0 } #-5.5
	

		#war-related economic malaise (WARDebt). The WARDebt will decrease over time if economic mobilization is reduced to minimum
		#maximum war debt penalty reaches -5.5% after about 5 consecutive years of total war mobilization
		#UK and France start out with high war debt. Germany low. USA/Italy/Japan medium.
		#USSR debt is a black box. Internal borrowing system is not quantified but should work roughly the same as any other country
		#Given its very limited ability to borrow externally, adding +90% debt to any USSR estimations.
		#command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 0 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 0    } #<30% debt to GDP (Germany 1936)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 3  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.1 } #30%  debt to GDP (Default new country)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 6  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.2 } #60%  debt to GDP (USA 1936; Italy 1936; Spain 1936; Japan 1936)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 9  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.3 } #90%  debt to GDP (USSR 1936)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 12 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.4 } #120% debt to GDP (USA 1946; Italy 1943)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 15 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.5 } #150% debt to GDP (UK 1936; France 1936)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 18 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.6 } #180% debt to GDP (USSR 1946)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 21 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.7 } #210% debt to GDP
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 24 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.8 } #240% debt to GDP (UK 1946; France 1946)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 27 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -0.9 } #270% debt to GDP (Germany 1946)
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 30 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1.0 } #300% debt to GDP
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 33 } } type = dissent value = 15  } #Country is bankrupt, can only fund itself by printing money, population is impoverished as a result
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 33 } } type = money value = -3000 } #The value of national currency collapses
		
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR2 } local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR3 } local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = WAR4 } local_flag = { which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR5  } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR6  } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR7  } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR8  } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR9  } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = WAR10 } type = local_setflag which = WARDebt when = 1 value = 1 }
		
		#war-related economic destruction (WARRuin).
		#WARRuin will increase when territory is lost/occupied, it will decrease over time when no territory is occupied 
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 5  } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 10 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 15 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 20 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 25 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 30 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 35 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 40 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -1 }
		
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 5  } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 10 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 15 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 20 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 25 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 30 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 35 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { lost_national = { value = 40 } } type = local_setflag which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 }
		
		#Cases where lost_national doesn't apply (i.e. civil war, collaborator puppet exists etc)
		#Spain will get all 4% per year, 12% if war ends in 1939
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = inMajorWar } type = industrial_modifier 	which = ic 				value = -4 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = inMajorWar } type = local_setflag 			which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 4 }
		
		#Recovering at 1% per year, if Spain takes a 12% hit, it will take 12 years to fully recover. If civil war ends sooner, it will take less
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 } NOT = { lost_national = { value = 2 } local_flag = inMajorWar } } type = industrial_modifier 	   	which = ic		value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = WARRuin when = 1 value = 1 } NOT = { lost_national = { value = 2 } local_flag = inMajorWar } } type = local_setflag when = 1		which = WARRuin	value = -1 }
		
		
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay1	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic		value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay1	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepPay1	value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec1	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier 		which = ic		value =  1 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec1	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepRec1	value = -1 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay2	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic		value = -2 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay2	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepPay2	value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec2	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier 		which = ic		value =  2 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec2	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepRec2	value = -1 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay3	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic		value = -3 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay3	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepPay3	value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec3	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier 		which = ic		value =  3 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec3	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepRec3	value = -1 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay4	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic		value = -4 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay4	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepPay4	value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec4	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier 		which = ic		value =  4 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec4	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepRec4	value = -1 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay5	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier		which = ic		value = -5 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepPay5	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepPay5	value = -1 } #Paying reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec5	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = industrial_modifier 		which = ic		value =  5 } #Receiving reparations
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = { which = RepRec5	when = 1 value = 1 } } type = local_setflag when = 1	which = RepRec5	value = -1 } #Receiving reparations
		
		#Sanctions shock/adjustment, delayed by one year
		command = { trigger = { OR = {  local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsAdj } local_flag = SanctionsDelay1 } type = industrial_modifier	which = ic	  value = -8 }
		command = { trigger = { OR = {  local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsAdj } local_flag = SanctionsDelay1 } type = local_setflag 		which = SanctionsAdj 	 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt 		  local_flag = SanctionsDelay1 } local_flag = SanctionsAdj } type = local_clrflag 		which = SanctionsDelay1  }
		command = { trigger = { OR = {  local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsAdj local_flag = SanctionsDelay1 } } type = local_setflag 		which = SanctionsDelay1  }
		#Sanctions lifted, rebounce delayed by one year
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } local_flag = SanctionsDelay2 local_flag = SanctionsAdj } 			 type = industrial_modifier	which = ic	  value = 8  }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } local_flag = SanctionsDelay2 local_flag = SanctionsAdj } 			 type = local_clrflag 		which = SanctionsAdj     }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt } local_flag = SanctionsDelay2 							 } 			 type = local_clrflag 		which = SanctionsDelay2  }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SanctionsWar local_flag = SanctionsEvt local_flag = SanctionsDelay2 } local_flag = SanctionsAdj } 			 type = local_setflag 		which = SanctionsDelay2  }
		#Sanctions persistent, -1% growth reduction per year
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = SanctionsAdj } 																									 type = industrial_modifier which = ic	  value = -1 }
		
		
		#Semi-Historical variance:
		
		#USSR historic growth rates 1935-1939: 15% 8% 10% 5% 8%
		#USSR base 2.5%, +4% growth with forced modernization, it also has a separate event chain for IC/infrastructure construction (150041). Builds +10 ic or approximately +3% over initial. Total: 9.5%
		command = { trigger = { country = SOV 						   } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = SOV local_flag = SOVAmbition } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 3  }
		
		#Spain historic growth rates 1935-1939: 2% -24% -7% 0% 10%
		#Partly covered by the WARRuin logic (-4% or more) + High Economic mobilization (-3.6%?) + Sanctions (-8%)
		#Spain's economic performance diverges significantly between Nationalist and Republican zones so will be covered separately.

		
		#China historic growth rates 1935-1939: 8% 6% -2% ?% ?%
		#Should be mostly covered by the poor country boost, but adding +1% also due to the enormous population potential. Same with India
		command = { trigger = { country = CHI } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = CHC } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = IND } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = U02 } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		
		#Germany historic growth rates 1935-1939: 8% 9% 11% 10% 9%
		#Mostly covered by Depression recovery and low sovereign debt. Adding +1% on top to match the historical rate of ~10%
		command = { trigger = { country = GER } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = DFR } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = DDR } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }
		command = { trigger = { country = U08 } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 1  }

		#Italy historic growth rates 1935-1939: 5% -4% 10% 3% 6%
		#Covered by sanctions adjustment/lifted
		#command = { trigger = { country = ITA year = 1936 NOT = { year = 1937 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = -8  }
		#command = { trigger = { country = ITA year = 1937 NOT = { year = 1938 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic value = 5   }
		
		#USA historic growth rates 1935-1939: 12% 10% 8% -6% 7%
		#Mostly covered by Depression recovery and low debt. Adding 1938 recession
		command = { trigger = { country = USA year = 1938 NOT = { year = 1939 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic  value = -14 }
		
		#France historic growth rates 1935-1939: -3% 4% 6% 0% 7%
		#Mostly covered by high sovereign debt, adding exceptionally good 1937/1939 and bad 1938 (probably fallout from US recession)
		command = { trigger = { country = FRA year = 1937 NOT = { year = 1938 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic  value = 3   }
		command = { trigger = { country = FRA year = 1938 NOT = { year = 1939 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic  value = -3  }
		command = { trigger = { country = FRA year = 1939 NOT = { year = 1940 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic  value = 4   }
		
		#UK historic growth rates 1935-1939: 4% 5% 3% 1% 1%
		#Covered by high sovereign debt and later lend lease boost
		
		#Japan historic growth rates 1935-1939: 4% 6% 4% 5% 14%
		#Covered by the poor country boost, adding exceptionally good 1939 (partially the delayed effect of the 1938 National General Mobilization Law?)
		command = { trigger = { country = JAP year = 1939 NOT = { year = 1940 } } type = industrial_modifier which = ic  value = 4   }

		command = { type = local_setflag which = EconomicGrowth when = 1 value = 1 }
	}
}

	id = 3012
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	#visible
	TAG = { AFG ALB ALG ANG ARA ARG ARM AST AUS AZB BEL BEN BHU BLR BOL BOS BRA BRU BUL BUR CAL CAM CAN CGX CHC CHI CHL CMB COL CON COS CRO CSA CSX CUB CXB CYN CYP CZE DDR DEN DFR DOM EAF ECU EGY ENG EQA EST ETH EUS FIN FLA FRA GAB GEO GER GLD GRE GUA GUI GUY HAI HOL HON HUN ICL IDC IND INO IRE IRQ ISR ITA JAP JOR KAZ KOR KUR KYG LAO LAT LBY LEB LIB LIT LUX MAD MAL MAN MEN MEX MLY MON MOR MOZ MTN NAM NEP NIC NIG NOR NZL OMN OTT PAK PAL PAN PAR PER PHI POL POR PRI PRK PRU QUE RHO ROM RSI RUS SAF SAL SAR SAU SCA SCH SCO SER SIA SIB SIE SIK SLO SLV SOM SOV SPA SPR SUD SWE SYR TAJ TAN TEX TIB TRA TRK TUN TUR UKR URU USA UZB VEN VIE WLL YEM YUG U01 U02 U03 U04 U05 U06 U08 U09 U10 U11 U12 U13 U14 U15 U16 U17 U18 U19 U20 U21 U22 U23 U24 U25 U26 U27 U28 U29 U30 U31 U32 U33 U34 U35 U36 U39 U40 U41 U42 U43 U44 U45 U46 U47 U48 U49 U50 U51 U52 U53 U54 U55 U56 U57 U58 U59 U60 U61 U62 U63 U64 U65 U66 U67 U68 U69 U70 U71 U72 U73 U74 U75 U76 U77 U78 U79 U80 U81 U82 U83 U84 U85 U86 U87 U88 U89 U90 U91 U92 U93 U94 U95 U96 U97 U98 U99 USN UIC UTL UAU UPS UCH UBO UCS URO UER UGS UPE UTC }
	
	name = "Supply shortages worsen"
	desc = "Our industry is proving to be woefully incapable of supplying our troops, resulting in many soldiers going to the front without rifles, without armor, without ammunition, and often without food. This situation is untenable and it is causing our armed forces to suffer increased casualties, rampant desertions, and mutinies. Some prominent commanders are threatening a vague 'March of Justice' by taking matters into their own hands! We must act now or our army will completely disintegrate!"
	picture = "mds_supplies2"
	style = 2
	
	action = {
		name = "Where's the ammunition!?!"
		trigger = {
			army = 5
			NOT = { supplies = 100 }
		}
		command = { type = dissent value = 1.0 } 
		command = { type = strength which = land 	when = 1 where = 0 value = -0.01 } #MP added back to MP pool
		command = { type = strength which = naval 	when = 1 where = 0 value = -0.01 } #MP added back to MP pool
		command = { type = strength which = air 	when = 1 where = 0 value = -0.01 } #MP added back to MP pool
		
		#will scrap the most obsolete or damaged units first
		command = { 																		type = demobilize which = land 	when = 0 where = 0 value = -3 } #MP added back to MP pool
		command = { trigger = { navy = { size = 3 type = 1 when = 0 where = 0 which = 0 } } type = demobilize which = naval when = 0 where = 0 value = -1 } #MP added back to MP pool
		command = { trigger = {  air = { size = 2 type = 1 when = 0 where = 0 which = 0 } } type = demobilize which = air  	when = 0 where = 0 value = -1 } #MP added back to MP pool
		
		command = { type = local_setflag which = shortagesCounter when = 1 value = 1 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = shortages }
		
		command = { type = event which = 3012 where = -1 when = 5 }
		command = { type = event which = 3013 where = -1 when = 5 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 3030
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	#invisible
	#Ideally, hawk lobby slider move events should handle this as well, but there are certain scenarios where they might not do it
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {	atwar = yes }
				policy = { type = democratic value = 2 }
			}
			AND = {
				atwar = yes
				NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	name = "War and Peace"
	desc = "This event helps override the hardcoded 50% Consumer Goods demand reduction from being at war"
	style = 2
	picture = "news_paper"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1913 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "War, what is it good for?"
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value = 10 } 													 } type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 10 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  9 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value = 10 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  9 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  8 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  9 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  8 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  7 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  8 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  7 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  6 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  7 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  6 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  5 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  6 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  5 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  4 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  5 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  4 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  3 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  4 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  3 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  2 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  3 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  2 }
		command = { trigger = { atwar = yes policy = { type = defense_lobby value =  1 } NOT = { policy = { type = democratic value =  2 } } } type = set_domestic which = democratic value =  2 }

Countries with low development level will tend to lag behind in research and will find it very difficult to build or upgrade modern weapons, be it tanks or warplanes. The result of all these investments is a military that is professional and able to punch considerably above its apparent weight and frequently surprise its opponents."

#War preparedness

event = {
	id = 3060
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	#invisible
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { local_flag = { which = war_preparedness when = 1 value = 1 } }
		atwar = yes
		#at war with a major opponent
		OR = {
			war = { country = GER }
			war = { country = JAP }
			war = { country = ITA }
			war = { country = USA }
			war = { country = SOV }
			war = { country = FRA }
			war = { country = ENG }
			war = { country = CHI }
		}
		NOT = { 
			AND = {
				alliance = { country = CHC }
				war = { country = CHI }
				NOT = {
					war = { country = JAP }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				alliance = { country = CHC }
				war = { country = JAP }
				NOT = {
					alliance = { country = CHI }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				war = { country = CHC } 
				NOT = {
					war = { country = CHI }
					war = { country = JAP }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					country = FRA
					country = ENG
					puppet = { country = -1 country = FRA }
					puppet = { country = -1 country = ENG }
				}
				war = { country = GER }
				NOT = {
					war = { country = BEL }
					alliance = { country = BEL }
					war = { country = SCH }
					alliance = { country = SCH }
					region = { region = "France" country = -2 data = 1 value = 1 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				war = { country = U87 } 
				NOT = {
					war = { country = CHI }
					war = { country = JAP }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country = USA
				war = { country = GER }
				flag = GER_USA_undeclared_war
			}
			AND = {
				alliance = { country = SOV }
				war = { country = JAP }
				flag = SOV_JAP_undeclared_war
			}
			AND = {
				alliance = { country = JAP }
				war = { country = SOV }
				flag = SOV_JAP_undeclared_war
			}
			AND = {
				alliance = { country = SOV }
				war = { country = ENG }
				war = { country = POL }
				NOT = { event =  2007019 }
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					country = FRA
					puppet = { country = -1 country = FRA }
				}
				war = { country = ENG }
				non_aggression = { country = FRA country = ENG }
			}
		}
	}
	
	name = "War preparedness"
	desc = "Despite our extensive preparations to face the enemy, when the war finally came to us, our military still turned out to be less prepared for a modern conflict than we would have liked to believe. Our troops were less organized than we thought and our officers of both senior and junior rank committed a number of embarassing errors during the opening phase of the conflict. This regrettably allowed the enemy to achieve some level of strategic surprise, and it took a few days before the situation began to normalize and our military effectiveness began to approach the levels we were hoping to see from the start. (Note that the strength and duration of the debuff is largely controlled by the 'militarism' level which determines military professionalism and peacetime readiness."

event = {
	id = 3061
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	#invisible
	
	name = "War preparedness"
	desc = "Despite our extensive preparations to face the enemy, when the war finally came to us, our military still turned out to be less prepared for a modern conflict than we would have liked to believe. Our troops were less organized than we thought and our officers of both senior and junior rank committed a number of embarassing errors during the opening phase of the conflict. This regrettably allowed the enemy to achieve some level of strategic surprise, and it took a few days before the situation began to normalize and our military effectiveness began to approach the levels we were hoping to see from the start. (Note that the strength and duration of the debuff is largely controlled by the 'militarism' level which determines military professionalism and peacetime readiness."

	picture = "news_paper"

#Stockpile reduction based on IC loss

event = {
	id = 3070
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	#invisible
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 10 } } 
					AND = {
						lost_IC = { value = 100 }
						NOT = { lost_national = { value = 10 } }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 1 } } 
							policy = { 	type = free_market 	value = 2 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 10 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 20 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 2 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 3 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 20 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 30 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 3 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 4 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 30 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 40 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 4 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 5 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 40 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 50 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 5 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 6 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 50 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 60 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 6 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 7 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 60 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 70 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 7 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 8 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 70 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 80 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 8 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 9 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				lost_IC = { value = 80 } 
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 90 } } 
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 9 } } 
							policy = {	type = free_market	value = 10 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					lost_IC = { value = 90 } 
					AND = {
						lost_IC = { value = 50 } 
						NOT = { ic = { value = 4 } }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = {	lost_IC = { value = 100 } }
					lost_national = { value = 10 }
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 10 } } 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	name = "Storage sites overrun"
	desc = "As enemy forces advance, they are overruning not just our factories by our fuel and grain silos, material wearhouses, and ammunition depots. We are making sure to blow up the contents of whatever resources we can't evacuate to deny it to the enemy, but alas, we also lose those resources which we worked so hard to accumulate."
	style = 2
	picture = "news_paper"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1913 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = march year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "No storage is lost"
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 10 } } 
				AND = {
					lost_IC = { value = 100 }
					NOT = { lost_national = { value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 1 } } 
						policy = { 	type = free_market 	value = 2 }
			}
		}
		command = { type = set_domestic which = free_market value = 1 }
	}
	action = {
		name = "10% of storage is lost"
		trigger = { 
			lost_IC = { value = 10 } 
			NOT = { lost_IC = { value = 20 } } 
			OR = {
				NOT = { policy = { 	type = free_market	value = 2 } }

			}
		}
		command = { type = set_domestic which = free_market value = 2 }

				lost_IC = { value = 90 }
